CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS daily_cases (
        date DATE PRIMARY KEY UNIQUE,
        url TEXT,
        local_cases TEXT,
        all_cases TEXT
    )
SELECT * FROM daily_cases ORDER BY date

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS daily_cases (
        date DATE PRIMARY KEY UNIQUE,
        url TEXT,
        local_cases TEXT,
        all_cases TEXT
    )
SELECT * FROM daily_cases ORDER BY date
